   pūrṇe pūrṇamanorathe vimukte jīvati rakṣa māṃ sarvopadravebhyaḥ svāhā /	pUrNe pUrNa manoraTe vimukte jIvati rakza mAm sarva upadraveByaH svAhA /
   sa mayūrapāśāṃś chitvā niṣpalānaḥ / kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau	sa mayUra pASAn CitvA nizpalAnaH / kim manyaDve BikzavaH yaH asO
   suvarṇāvabhāso nāma mayūrarājas tena kālena tena samayena / tadāpi mama	suvarNa avaBAsaH nAma mayUra rAjaH tena kAlena tena samayena / tadA api mama
   mahāmāyūrī vidyā upakarā ca bahukarā ca etarhy api mama mahāmāyūrī vidyā	mahAmAyUrI vidyA upakarA ca bahu karA ca etarhi api mama mahAmAyUrI vidyA
   upakarā ca bahukarā ceti / paśya bhadanta yāvac ca bhagavataḥ svāter	upakarA ca bahu karA ca iti / paSya Badanta yAvat ca BagavataH svAteH 
   bhikṣor vidyayā svastyayanaṃ kṛtam* / na bhikṣava etarhi yathātīte 'py	BikzoH vidyayA svastyayanam kRtam* / na BikzavaH etarhi yaTA atIte api 
   adhvani / tac chrūyatām* /	aDvani / tat SrUyatAm* /
   bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ nāgamaṇḍaliko 'nyatamaḥ	BUta pUrvam BikzavaH vArANasyAm nagaryAm nAgamaNxalikaH anyatamaH
   kṣatriyadārakaḥ sarpeṇa dṛṣṭaḥ / sa kālagataḥ / nāgamaṇḍalikena vidyayā	kzatriya dArakaH sarpeNa dRzwaH / sa kAlagataH / nAga maNxalikena vidyayA
   tasya svāsthyaṃ kṛtam* / kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau nāgamaṇḍalikaḥ	tasya svAsTyam kRtam* / kim manyaDve BikzavaH yaH asO nAgamaNxalikaH
   ahaṃ sa tena kālena tena samayena / yo 'sau dārakaḥ svātir bhikṣus tena	aham sa tena kAlena tena samayena / yaH asO dArakaH svAtiH BikzuH tena
   kālena tena samayena /	kAlena tena samayena /
   bhaiṣajyavastu samāptam* //	BEzajya vastu samAptam* //
